<h2 id="examples" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#examples"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Examples</h2>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_4bhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_4bhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_4bhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="controlled" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#controlled"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Controlled</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">When using the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">RatingGroup</code> component, you can use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">value</code> and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">onValueChange</code> props to control the state.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_4hhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_4hhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_4hhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="root-provider" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#root-provider"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Root Provider</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">An alternative way to control the rating group is to use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">RootProvider</code> component and the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">useRatingGroup</code> hook.
This way you can access the state and methods from outside the component.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_4nhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_4nhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_4nhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="field" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#field"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Field</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">The <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Field</code> component helps manage form-related state and accessibility attributes of a rating group. It includes
handling ARIA labels, helper text, and error text to ensure proper accessibility.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_4thanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_4thanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_4thanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="half-rating" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#half-rating"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Half Rating</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Allow <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">0.5</code> value steps by setting the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">allowHalf</code> prop to <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">true</code>. Ensure to render the correct icon if the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">half</code> value
is set in the Rating components render callback.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_53hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_53hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_53hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="forms" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#forms"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Forms</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">To use the rating group within forms, pass the prop <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">name</code>. It will render a hidden input and ensure the value changes
get propagated to the form correctly.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_59hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_59hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_59hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="disabled" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#disabled"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Disabled</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">To make the rating group disabled, set the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">disabled</code> prop to <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">true</code>.</p>

<h2 id="api-reference" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#api-reference"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>API Reference</h2>
<h3 id="props" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#props"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Props</h3>

<h2 id="accessibility" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#accessibility"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Accessibility</h2>
<h3 id="keyboard-support" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#keyboard-support"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Keyboard Support</h3>
<div class="bd-w_1px bdr_lg ov-x_auto not-prose"><table class="bd_0 table__root table__root--size_sm table__root--variant_outline"><thead class="table__head table__head--size_sm /\u003e\n\n## Anatomy\n\n\u003cAnatomy id=\"rating-group\" /\u003e\n\n```tsx\n\u003cRatingGroup.Root\u003e\n  \u003cRatingGroup.Label /\u003e\n  \u003cRatingGroup.Control\u003e\n    \u003cRatingGroup.Item\u003e\n      \u003cRatingGroup.ItemContext /\u003e\n    \u003c/RatingGroup.Item\u003e\n    \u003cRatingGroup.HiddenInput /\u003e\n  \u003c/RatingGroup.Control\u003e\n\u003c/RatingGroup.Root\u003e\n```\n\n## Examples\n\n**Example: basic**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { RatingGroup } from '@ark-ui/react/rating-group'\nimport { \u003cRatingGroup.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/RatingGroup.Label\u003e\n    \u003cRatingGroup.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n      \u003cRatingGroup.Context\u003e\n '' : undefined}\u003e\n                      \u003cStarIcon data-bg=\"\" /\u003e\n                      \u003cStarIcon data-fg=\"\" fill=\"currentColor\" /\u003e\n                    \u003c/span\u003e\n                  )}\n                \u003c/RatingGroup.ItemContext\u003e\n              \u003c/RatingGroup.Item\u003e\n            )}\n          \u003c/Index\u003e\n        )}\n      \u003c/RatingGroup.Context\u003e\n      \u003cRatingGroup.HiddenInput /\u003e\n    \u003c/RatingGroup.Control\u003e\n  \u003c/RatingGroup.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { RatingGroup } from '@ark-ui/vue/rating-group'\nimport { StarIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport styles from 'styles/rating-group.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cRatingGroup.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" :default-value=\"3\"\u003e\n    \u003cRatingGroup.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003eLabel\u003c/RatingGroup.Label\u003e\n    \u003cRatingGroup.Control :class=\"styles.Control\"\u003e\n      \u003cRatingGroup.Context v-slot=\"{ items }\"\u003e\n        \u003cRatingGroup.Item v-for=\"item in items\" :key=\"item\" :class=\"styles.Item\" :index=\"item\"\u003e\n          \u003cRatingGroup.ItemContext v-slot=\"{ highlighted }\"\u003e\n            \u003cspan :class=\"styles.ItemIndicator\" :data-highlighted=\"highlighted ? '' : undefined\"\u003e\n              \u003cStarIcon data-bg=\"\" /\u003e\n              \u003cStarIcon data-fg=\"\" fill=\"currentColor\" /\u003e\n            \u003c/span\u003e\n          \u003c/RatingGroup.ItemContext\u003e\n        \u003c/RatingGroup.Item\u003e\n      \u003c/RatingGroup.Context\u003e\n      \u003cRatingGroup.HiddenInput /\u003e\n    \u003c/RatingGroup.Control\u003e\n  \u003c/RatingGroup.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { RatingGroup } from '@ark-ui/svelte/rating-group'\n  import { StarIcon } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import styles from 'styles/rating-group.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cRatingGroup.Root class={styles.Root} defaultValue={3}\u003e\n  \u003cRatingGroup.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/RatingGroup.Label\u003e\n  \u003cRatingGroup.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n    \u003cRatingGroup.Context\u003e\n      {#snippet render(ratingGroup)}\n        {#each ratingGroup().items as item}\n          \u003cRatingGroup.Item class={styles.Item} index={item}\u003e\n            \u003cRatingGroup.ItemContext\u003e\n              {#snippet render(itemState)}\n                \u003cspan class={styles.ItemIndicator} data-highlighted={itemState().highlighted ? '' : undefined}\u003e\n                  \u003cStarIcon data-bg=\"\" /\u003e\n                  \u003cStarIcon data-fg=\"\" fill=\"currentColor\" /\u003e\n                \u003c/span\u003e\n              {/snippet}\n            \u003c/RatingGroup.ItemContext\u003e\n          \u003c/RatingGroup.Item\u003e\n        {/each}\n      {/snippet}\n    \u003c/RatingGroup.Context\u003e\n    \u003cRatingGroup.HiddenInput /\u003e\n  \u003c/RatingGroup.Control\u003e\n\u003c/RatingGroup.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Controlled\n\nWhen using the `RatingGroup` component, you can use the `value` and `onValueChange` props to control the state.\n\n**Example: controlled**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { RatingGroup } from '@ark-ui/react/rating-group'\nimport { StarIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport { useState } from 'react'\nimport styles from 'styles/rating-group.module.css'\n\nexport const Controlled = () =\u003e {\n  const [value, setValue] = useState(0)\n\n  return (\n    \u003cRatingGroup.Root className={styles.Root} value={value} onValueChange={(details) =\u003e setValue(details.value)}\u003e\n      \u003cRatingGroup.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/RatingGroup.Label\u003e\n      \u003cRatingGroup.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cRatingGroup.Context\u003e\n          {({ items }) =\u003e\n            items.map((item) =\u003e (\n              \u003cRatingGroup.Item className={styles.Item} key={item} index={item}\u003e\n                \u003cRatingGroup.ItemContext\u003e\n                  {({ half, highlighted }) =\u003e (\n                    \u003cspan\n                      className={styles.ItemIndicator}\n                      data-half={half ? '' : undefined}\n                      data-highlighted={highlighted ? '' : undefined}\n                    \u003e\n                      \u003cStarIcon data-bg=\"\" /\u003e\n                      \u003cStarIcon data-fg=\"\" fill=\"currentColor\" /\u003e\n                    \u003c/span\u003e\n                  )}\n                \u003c/RatingGroup.ItemContext\u003e\n              \u003c/RatingGroup.Item\u003e\n            ))\n          }\n        \u003c/RatingGroup.Context\u003e\n        \u003cRatingGroup.HiddenInput /\u003e\n      \u003c/RatingGroup.Control\u003e\n    \u003c/RatingGroup.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { RatingGroup } from '@ark-ui/solid/rating-group'\nimport { StarIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { Index, createSignal } from 'solid-js'\nimport styles from 'styles/rating-group.module.css'\n\nexport const Controlled = () =\u003e {\n  const [value, setValue] = createSignal(0)\n\n  return (\n    \u003cRatingGroup.Root class={styles.Root} value={value()} onValueChange={(details) =\u003e setValue(details.value)}\u003e\n      \u003cRatingGroup.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/RatingGroup.Label\u003e\n      \u003cRatingGroup.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cRatingGroup.Context\u003e\n          {(context) =\u003e (\n            \u003cIndex each={context().items}\u003e\n              {(item) =\u003e (\n                \u003cRatingGroup.Item class={styles.Item} index={item()}\u003e\n                  \u003cRatingGroup.ItemContext\u003e\n                    {(itemContext) =\u003e (\n                      \u003cspan\n                        class={styles.ItemIndicator}\n                        data-half={itemContext().half ? '' : undefined}\n                        data-highlighted={itemContext().highlighted ? '' : undefined}\n                      \u003e\n                        \u003cStarIcon data-bg=\"\" /\u003e\n                        \u003cStarIcon data-fg=\"\" fill=\"currentColor\" /\u003e\n                      \u003c/span\u003e\n                    )}\n                  \u003c/RatingGroup.ItemContext\u003e\n                \u003c/RatingGroup.Item\u003e\n              )}\n            \u003c/Index\u003e\n          )}\n        \u003c/RatingGroup.Context\u003e\n        \u003cRatingGroup.HiddenInput /\u003e\n      \u003c/RatingGroup.Control\u003e\n    \u003c/RatingGroup.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { RatingGroup } from '@ark-ui/vue/rating-group'\nimport { StarIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport { ref } from 'vue'\nimport styles from 'styles/rating-group.module.css'\n\nconst value = ref(0)\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cRatingGroup.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" v-model=\"value\"\u003e\n    \u003cRatingGroup.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003eLabel\u003c/RatingGroup.Label\u003e\n    \u003cRatingGroup.Control :class=\"styles.Control\"\u003e\n      \u003cRatingGroup.Context v-slot=\"{ items }\"\u003e\n        \u003cRatingGroup.Item v-for=\"item in items\" :key=\"item\" :class=\"styles.Item\" :index=\"item\"\u003e\n          \u003cRatingGroup.ItemContext v-slot=\"{ half, highlighted }\"\u003e\n            \u003cspan\n              :class=\"styles.ItemIndicator\"\n              :data-half=\"half ? '' : undefined\"\n              :data-highlighted=\"highlighted ? '' : undefined\"\n            \u003e\n              \u003cStarIcon data-bg=\"\" /\u003e\n              \u003cStarIcon data-fg=\"\" fill=\"currentColor\" /\u003e\n            \u003c/span\u003e\n          \u003c/RatingGroup.ItemContext\u003e\n        \u003c/RatingGroup.Item\u003e\n      \u003c/RatingGroup.Context\u003e\n      \u003cRatingGroup.HiddenInput /\u003e\n    \u003c/RatingGroup.Control\u003e\n  \u003c/RatingGroup.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { RatingGroup } from '@ark-ui/svelte/rating-group'\n  import { StarIcon } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import styles from 'styles/rating-group.module.css'\n\n  let value = $state(0)\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cRatingGroup.Root class={styles.Root} bind:value\u003e\n  \u003cRatingGroup.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/RatingGroup.Label\u003e\n  \u003cRatingGroup.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n    \u003cRatingGroup.Context\u003e\n      {#snippet render(ratingGroup)}\n        {#each ratingGroup().items as item}\n          \u003cRatingGroup.Item class={styles.Item} index={item}\u003e\n            \u003cRatingGroup.ItemContext\u003e\n              {#snippet render(itemState)}\n                \u003cspan\n                  class={styles.ItemIndicator}\n                  data-half={itemState().half ? '' : undefined}\n                  data-highlighted={itemState().highlighted ? '' : undefined}\n                \u003e\n                  \u003cStarIcon data-bg=\"\" /\u003e\n                  \u003cStarIcon data-fg=\"\" fill=\"currentColor\" /\u003e\n                \u003c/span\u003e\n              {/snippet}\n            \u003c/RatingGroup.ItemContext\u003e\n          \u003c/RatingGroup.Item\u003e\n        {/each}\n      {/snippet}\n    \u003c/RatingGroup.Context\u003e\n    \u003cRatingGroup.HiddenInput /\u003e\n  \u003c/RatingGroup.Control\u003e\n\u003c/RatingGroup.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Root Provider\n\nAn alternative way to control the rating group is to use the `RootProvider` component and the `useRatingGroup` hook.\nThis way you can access the state and methods from outside the component.\n\n**Example: root-provider**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { RatingGroup, useRatingGroup } from '@ark-ui/react/rating-group'\nimport { StarIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport styles from 'styles/rating-group.module.css'\n\nexport const RootProvider = () =\u003e {\n  const ratingGroup = useRatingGroup({ count: 5, defaultValue: 3 })\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv className=\"stack\"\u003e\n      \u003coutput\u003evalue: {ratingGroup.value}\u003c/output\u003e\n      \u003cRatingGroup.RootProvider className={styles.Root} value={ratingGroup}\u003e\n        \u003cRatingGroup.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/RatingGroup.Label\u003e\n        \u003cRatingGroup.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n          \u003cRatingGroup.Context\u003e\n            {({ items }) =\u003e\n              items.map((item) =\u003e (\n                \u003cRatingGroup.Item className={styles.Item} key={item} index={item}\u003e\n                  \u003cRatingGroup.ItemContext\u003e\n                    {({ highlighted }) =\u003e (\n                      \u003cspan className={styles.ItemIndicator} data-highlighted={highlighted ? '' : undefined}\u003e\n                        \u003cStarIcon data-bg=\"\" /\u003e\n                        \u003cStarIcon data-fg=\"\" fill=\"currentColor\" /\u003e\n                      \u003c/span\u003e\n                    )}\n                  \u003c/RatingGroup.ItemContext\u003e\n                \u003c/RatingGroup.Item\u003e\n              ))\n            }\n          \u003c/RatingGroup.Context\u003e\n          \u003cRatingGroup.HiddenInput /\u003e\n        \u003c/RatingGroup.Control\u003e\n      \u003c/RatingGroup.RootProvider\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { RatingGroup, useRatingGroup } from '@ark-ui/solid/rating-group'\nimport { StarIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { Index } from 'solid-js'\nimport styles from 'styles/rating-group.module.css'\n\nexport const RootProvider = () =\u003e {\n  const ratingGroup = useRatingGroup({ defaultValue: 3 })\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv class=\"stack\"\u003e\n      \u003coutput\u003evalue: {ratingGroup().value}\u003c/output\u003e\n      \u003cRatingGroup.RootProvider class={styles.Root} value={ratingGroup}\u003e\n        \u003cRatingGroup.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/RatingGroup.Label\u003e\n        \u003cRatingGroup.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n          \u003cRatingGroup.Context\u003e\n            {(context) =\u003e (\n              \u003cIndex each={context().items}\u003e\n                {(item) =\u003e (\n                  \u003cRatingGroup.Item class={styles.Item} index={item()}\u003e\n                    \u003cRatingGroup.ItemContext\u003e\n                      {(itemContext) =\u003e (\n                        \u003cspan\n                          class={styles.ItemIndicator}\n                          data-highlighted={itemContext().highlighted ? '' : undefined}\n                        \u003e\n                          \u003cStarIcon data-bg=\"\" /\u003e\n                          \u003cStarIcon data-fg=\"\" fill=\"currentColor\" /\u003e\n                        \u003c/span\u003e\n                      )}\n                    \u003c/RatingGroup.ItemContext\u003e\n                  \u003c/RatingGroup.Item\u003e\n                )}\n              \u003c/Index\u003e\n            )}\n          \u003c/RatingGroup.Context\u003e\n          \u003cRatingGroup.HiddenInput /\u003e\n        \u003c/RatingGroup.Control\u003e\n      \u003c/RatingGroup.RootProvider\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { RatingGroup, useRatingGroup } from '@ark-ui/vue/rating-group'\nimport { StarIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport styles from 'styles/rating-group.module.css'\n\nconst ratingGroup = useRatingGroup({ defaultValue: 3 })\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cdiv class=\"stack\"\u003e\n    \u003coutput\u003evalue: {{ ratingGroup.value }}\u003c/output\u003e\n    \u003cRatingGroup.RootProvider :class=\"styles.Root\" :value=\"ratingGroup\"\u003e\n      \u003cRatingGroup.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003eLabel\u003c/RatingGroup.Label\u003e\n      \u003cRatingGroup.Control :class=\"styles.Control\"\u003e\n        \u003cRatingGroup.Context v-slot=\"{ items }\"\u003e\n          \u003cRatingGroup.Item v-for=\"item in items\" :key=\"item\" :class=\"styles.Item\" :index=\"item\"\u003e\n            \u003cRatingGroup.ItemContext v-slot=\"{ highlighted }\"\u003e\n              \u003cspan :class=\"styles.ItemIndicator\" :data-highlighted=\"highlighted ? '' : undefined\"\u003e\n                \u003cStarIcon data-bg=\"\" /\u003e\n                \u003cStarIcon data-fg=\"\" fill=\"currentColor\" /\u003e\n              \u003c/span\u003e\n            \u003c/RatingGroup.ItemContext\u003e\n          \u003c/RatingGroup.Item\u003e\n        \u003c/RatingGroup.Context\u003e\n        \u003cRatingGroup.HiddenInput /\u003e\n      \u003c/RatingGroup.Control\u003e\n    \u003c/RatingGroup.RootProvider\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { RatingGroup, useRatingGroup } from '@ark-ui/svelte/rating-group'\n  import { StarIcon } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import styles from 'styles/rating-group.module.css'\n\n  const id = $props.id()\n  const ratingGroup = useRatingGroup({ id, defaultValue: 3 })\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cdiv class=\"stack\"\u003e\n  \u003coutput\u003evalue: {ratingGroup().value}\u003c/output\u003e\n  \u003cRatingGroup.RootProvider class={styles.Root} value={ratingGroup}\u003e\n    \u003cRatingGroup.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/RatingGroup.Label\u003e\n    \u003cRatingGroup.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n      \u003cRatingGroup.Context\u003e\n        {#snippet render(context)}\n          {#each context().items as item}\n            \u003cRatingGroup.Item class={styles.Item} index={item}\u003e\n              \u003cRatingGroup.ItemContext\u003e\n                {#snippet render(itemState)}\n                  \u003cspan class={styles.ItemIndicator} data-highlighted={itemState().highlighted ? '' : undefined}\u003e\n                    \u003cStarIcon data-bg=\"\" /\u003e\n                    \u003cStarIcon data-fg=\"\" fill=\"currentColor\" /\u003e\n                  \u003c/span\u003e\n                {/snippet}\n              \u003c/RatingGroup.ItemContext\u003e\n            \u003c/RatingGroup.Item\u003e\n          {/each}\n        {/snippet}\n      \u003c/RatingGroup.Context\u003e\n      \u003cRatingGroup.HiddenInput /\u003e\n    \u003c/RatingGroup.Control\u003e\n  \u003c/RatingGroup.RootProvider\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Field\n\nThe `Field` component helps manage form-related state and accessibility attributes of a rating group. It includes\nhandling ARIA labels, helper text, and error text to ensure proper accessibility.\n\n**Example: with-field**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Field } from '@ark-ui/react/field'\nimport { RatingGroup } from '@ark-ui/react/rating-group'\nimport { StarIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport field from 'styles/field.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/rating-group.module.css'\n\nexport const WithField = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cField.Root className={field.Root}\u003e\n    \u003cRatingGroup.Root className={styles.Root} count={5} defaultValue={3}\u003e\n      \u003cRatingGroup.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/RatingGroup.Label\u003e\n      \u003cRatingGroup.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cRatingGroup.Context\u003e\n          {({ items }) =\u003e\n            items.map((item) =\u003e (\n              \u003cRatingGroup.Item className={styles.Item} key={item} index={item}\u003e\n                \u003cRatingGroup.ItemContext\u003e\n                  {({ highlighted }) =\u003e (\n                    \u003cspan className={styles.ItemIndicator} data-highlighted={highlighted ? '' : undefined}\u003e\n                      \u003cStarIcon data-bg=\"\" /\u003e\n                      \u003cStarIcon data-fg=\"\" fill=\"currentColor\" /\u003e\n                    \u003c/span\u003e\n                  )}\n                \u003c/RatingGroup.ItemContext\u003e\n              \u003c/RatingGroup.Item\u003e\n            ))\n          }\n        \u003c/RatingGroup.Context\u003e\n        \u003cRatingGroup.HiddenInput /\u003e\n      \u003c/RatingGroup.Control\u003e\n    \u003c/RatingGroup.Root\u003e\n    \u003cField.HelperText className={field.HelperText}\u003eAdditional Info\u003c/Field.HelperText\u003e\n    \u003cField.ErrorText className={field.ErrorText}\u003eError Info\u003c/Field.ErrorText\u003e\n  \u003c/Field.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Field } from '@ark-ui/solid/field'\nimport { RatingGroup } from '@ark-ui/solid/rating-group'\nimport { StarIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { Index } from 'solid-js'\nimport field from 'styles/field.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/rating-group.module.css'\n\nexport const WithField = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cField.Root class={field.Root}\u003e\n    \u003cRatingGroup.Root class={styles.Root} defaultValue={3}\u003e\n      \u003cRatingGroup.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/RatingGroup.Label\u003e\n      \u003cRatingGroup.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cRatingGroup.Context\u003e\n          {(context) =\u003e (\n            \u003cIndex each={context().items}\u003e\n              {(item) =\u003e (\n                \u003cRatingGroup.Item class={styles.Item} index={item()}\u003e\n                  \u003cRatingGroup.ItemContext\u003e\n                    {(itemContext) =\u003e (\n                      \u003cspan class={styles.ItemIndicator} data-highlighted={itemContext().highlighted ? '' : undefined}\u003e\n                        \u003cStarIcon data-bg=\"\" /\u003e\n                        \u003cStarIcon data-fg=\"\" fill=\"currentColor\" /\u003e\n                      \u003c/span\u003e\n                    )}\n                  \u003c/RatingGroup.ItemContext\u003e\n                \u003c/RatingGroup.Item\u003e\n              )}\n            \u003c/Index\u003e\n          )}\n        \u003c/RatingGroup.Context\u003e\n        \u003cRatingGroup.HiddenInput /\u003e\n      \u003c/RatingGroup.Control\u003e\n    \u003c/RatingGroup.Root\u003e\n    \u003cField.HelperText class={field.HelperText}\u003eAdditional Info\u003c/Field.HelperText\u003e\n    \u003cField.ErrorText class={field.ErrorText}\u003eError Info\u003c/Field.ErrorText\u003e\n  \u003c/Field.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Field } from '@ark-ui/vue/field'\nimport { RatingGroup } from '@ark-ui/vue/rating-group'\nimport { StarIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport field from 'styles/field.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/rating-group.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cField.Root :class=\"field.Root\"\u003e\n    \u003cRatingGroup.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" :default-value=\"3\"\u003e\n      \u003cRatingGroup.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003eLabel\u003c/RatingGroup.Label\u003e\n      \u003cRatingGroup.Control :class=\"styles.Control\"\u003e\n        \u003cRatingGroup.Context v-slot=\"{ items }\"\u003e\n          \u003cRatingGroup.Item v-for=\"item in items\" :key=\"item\" :class=\"styles.Item\" :index=\"item\"\u003e\n            \u003cRatingGroup.ItemContext v-slot=\"{ highlighted }\"\u003e\n              \u003cspan :class=\"styles.ItemIndicator\" :data-highlighted=\"highlighted ? '' : undefined\"\u003e\n                \u003cStarIcon data-bg=\"\" /\u003e\n                \u003cStarIcon data-fg=\"\" fill=\"currentColor\" /\u003e\n              \u003c/span\u003e\n            \u003c/RatingGroup.ItemContext\u003e\n          \u003c/RatingGroup.Item\u003e\n        \u003c/RatingGroup.Context\u003e\n        \u003cRatingGroup.HiddenInput /\u003e\n      \u003c/RatingGroup.Control\u003e\n    \u003c/RatingGroup.Root\u003e\n    \u003cField.HelperText :class=\"field.HelperText\"\u003eAdditional Info\u003c/Field.HelperText\u003e\n    \u003cField.ErrorText :class=\"field.ErrorText\"\u003eError Info\u003c/Field.ErrorText\u003e\n  \u003c/Field.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Field } from '@ark-ui/svelte/field'\n  import { RatingGroup } from '@ark-ui/svelte/rating-group'\n  import { StarIcon } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import field from 'styles/field.module.css'\n  import styles from 'styles/rating-group.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cField.Root class={field.Root}\u003e\n  \u003cRatingGroup.Root class={styles.Root} defaultValue={3}\u003e\n    \u003cRatingGroup.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/RatingGroup.Label\u003e\n    \u003cRatingGroup.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n      \u003cRatingGroup.Context\u003e\n        {#snippet render(ratingGroup)}\n          {#each ratingGroup().items as item}\n            \u003cRatingGroup.Item class={styles.Item} index={item}\u003e\n              \u003cRatingGroup.ItemContext\u003e\n                {#snippet render(itemState)}\n                  \u003cspan class={styles.ItemIndicator} data-highlighted={itemState().highlighted ? '' : undefined}\u003e\n                    \u003cStarIcon data-bg=\"\" /\u003e\n                    \u003cStarIcon data-fg=\"\" fill=\"currentColor\" /\u003e\n                  \u003c/span\u003e\n                {/snippet}\n              \u003c/RatingGroup.ItemContext\u003e\n            \u003c/RatingGroup.Item\u003e\n          {/each}\n        {/snippet}\n      \u003c/RatingGroup.Context\u003e\n      \u003cRatingGroup.HiddenInput /\u003e\n    \u003c/RatingGroup.Control\u003e\n  \u003c/RatingGroup.Root\u003e\n  \u003cField.HelperText class={field.HelperText}\u003eAdditional Info\u003c/Field.HelperText\u003e\n  \u003cField.ErrorText class={field.ErrorText}\u003eError Info\u003c/Field.ErrorText\u003e\n\u003c/Field.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Half Rating\n\nAllow `0.5` value steps by setting the `allowHalf` prop to `true`. Ensure to render the correct icon if the `half` value\nis set in the Rating components render callback.\n\n**Example: half-star**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { RatingGroup } from '@ark-ui/react/rating-group'\nimport { StarIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport styles from 'styles/rating-group.module.css'\n\nexport const HalfStar = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cRatingGroup.Root className={styles.Root} defaultValue={2.5} allowHalf\u003e\n    \u003cRatingGroup.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/RatingGroup.Label\u003e\n    \u003cRatingGroup.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n      \u003cRatingGroup.Context\u003e\n        {({ items }) =\u003e\n          items.map((item) =\u003e (\n            \u003cRatingGroup.Item className={styles.Item} key={item} index={item}\u003e\n              \u003cRatingGroup.ItemContext\u003e\n                {({ half, highlighted }) =\u003e (\n                  \u003cspan\n                    className={styles.ItemIndicator}\n                    data-half={half ? '' : undefined}\n                    data-highlighted={highlighted ? '' : undefined}\n                  \u003e\n                    \u003cStarIcon data-bg=\"\" /\u003e\n                    \u003cStarIcon data-fg=\"\" fill=\"currentColor\" /\u003e\n                  \u003c/span\u003e\n                )}\n              \u003c/RatingGroup.ItemContext\u003e\n            \u003c/RatingGroup.Item\u003e\n          ))\n        }\n      \u003c/RatingGroup.Context\u003e\n      \u003cRatingGroup.HiddenInput /\u003e\n    \u003c/RatingGroup.Control\u003e\n  \u003c/RatingGroup.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { RatingGroup } from '@ark-ui/solid/rating-group'\nimport { StarIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { Index } from 'solid-js'\nimport styles from 'styles/rating-group.module.css'\n\nexport const HalfStar = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cRatingGroup.Root class={styles.Root} defaultValue={2.5} allowHalf\u003e\n    \u003cRatingGroup.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/RatingGroup.Label\u003e\n    \u003cRatingGroup.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n      \u003cRatingGroup.Context\u003e\n        {(context) =\u003e (\n          \u003cIndex each={context().items}\u003e\n            {(item) =\u003e (\n              \u003cRatingGroup.Item class={styles.Item} index={item()}\u003e\n                \u003cRatingGroup.ItemContext\u003e\n                  {(itemContext) =\u003e (\n                    \u003cspan\n                      class={styles.ItemIndicator}\n                      data-half={itemContext().half ? '' : undefined}\n                      data-highlighted={itemContext().highlighted ? '' : undefined}\n                    \u003e\n                      \u003cStarIcon data-bg=\"\" /\u003e\n                      \u003cStarIcon data-fg=\"\" fill=\"currentColor\" /\u003e\n                    \u003c/span\u003e\n                  )}\n                \u003c/RatingGroup.ItemContext\u003e\n              \u003c/RatingGroup.Item\u003e\n            )}\n          \u003c/Index\u003e\n        )}\n      \u003c/RatingGroup.Context\u003e\n      \u003cRatingGroup.HiddenInput /\u003e\n    \u003c/RatingGroup.Control\u003e\n  \u003c/RatingGroup.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { RatingGroup } from '@ark-ui/vue/rating-group'\nimport { StarIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport styles from 'styles/rating-group.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cRatingGroup.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" :default-value=\"2.5\" allow-half\u003e\n    \u003cRatingGroup.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003eLabel\u003c/RatingGroup.Label\u003e\n    \u003cRatingGroup.Control :class=\"styles.Control\"\u003e\n      \u003cRatingGroup.Context v-slot=\"{ items }\"\u003e\n        \u003cRatingGroup.Item v-for=\"item in items\" :key=\"item\" :class=\"styles.Item\" :index=\"item\"\u003e\n          \u003cRatingGroup.ItemContext v-slot=\"{ half, highlighted }\"\u003e\n            \u003cspan\n              :class=\"styles.ItemIndicator\"\n              :data-half=\"half ? '' : undefined\"\n              :data-highlighted=\"highlighted ? '' : undefined\"\n            \u003e\n              \u003cStarIcon data-bg=\"\" /\u003e\n              \u003cStarIcon data-fg=\"\" fill=\"currentColor\" /\u003e\n            \u003c/span\u003e\n          \u003c/RatingGroup.ItemContext\u003e\n        \u003c/RatingGroup.Item\u003e\n      \u003c/RatingGroup.Context\u003e\n      \u003cRatingGroup.HiddenInput /\u003e\n    \u003c/RatingGroup.Control\u003e\n  \u003c/RatingGroup.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { RatingGroup } from '@ark-ui/svelte/rating-group'\n  import { StarIcon } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import styles from 'styles/rating-group.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cRatingGroup.Root class={styles.Root} defaultValue={2.5} allowHalf\u003e\n  \u003cRatingGroup.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/RatingGroup.Label\u003e\n  \u003cRatingGroup.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n    \u003cRatingGroup.Context\u003e\n      {#snippet render(ratingGroup)}\n        {#each ratingGroup().items as item}\n          \u003cRatingGroup.Item class={styles.Item} index={item}\u003e\n            \u003cRatingGroup.ItemContext\u003e\n              {#snippet render(itemState)}\n                \u003cspan\n                  class={styles.ItemIndicator}\n                  data-half={itemState().half ? '' : undefined}\n                  data-highlighted={itemState().highlighted ? '' : undefined}\n                \u003e\n                  \u003cStarIcon data-bg=\"\" /\u003e\n                  \u003cStarIcon data-fg=\"\" fill=\"currentColor\" /\u003e\n                \u003c/span\u003e\n              {/snippet}\n            \u003c/RatingGroup.ItemContext\u003e\n          \u003c/RatingGroup.Item\u003e\n        {/each}\n      {/snippet}\n    \u003c/RatingGroup.Context\u003e\n    \u003cRatingGroup.HiddenInput /\u003e\n  \u003c/RatingGroup.Control\u003e\n\u003c/RatingGroup.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Forms\n\nTo use the rating group within forms, pass the prop `name`. It will render a hidden input and ensure the value changes\nget propagated to the form correctly.\n\n**Example: form-usage**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { RatingGroup } from '@ark-ui/react/rating-group'\nimport { StarIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport styles from 'styles/rating-group.module.css'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\n\nexport const FormUsage = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cform\n    className=\"stack\"\n    onSubmit={(e) =\u003e {\n      e.preventDefault()\n      const formData = new FormData(e.currentTarget)\n      alert(`Rating value: ${formData.get('review')}`)\n    }}\n  \u003e\n    \u003cRatingGroup.Root className={styles.Root} name=\"review\" defaultValue={3}\u003e\n      \u003cRatingGroup.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/RatingGroup.Label\u003e\n      \u003cRatingGroup.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n        \u003cRatingGroup.Context\u003e\n          {({ items }) =\u003e\n            items.map((item) =\u003e (\n              \u003cRatingGroup.Item className={styles.Item} key={item} index={item}\u003e\n                \u003cRatingGroup.ItemContext\u003e\n                  {({ highlighted }) =\u003e (\n                    \u003cspan className={styles.ItemIndicator} data-highlighted={highlighted ? '' : undefined}\u003e\n                      \u003cStarIcon data-bg=\"\" /\u003e\n                      \u003cStarIcon data-fg=\"\" fill=\"currentColor\" /\u003e\n                    \u003c/span\u003e\n                  )}\n                \u003c/RatingGroup.ItemContext\u003e\n              \u003c/RatingGroup.Item\u003e\n            ))\n          }\n        \u003c/RatingGroup.Context\u003e\n        \u003cRatingGroup.HiddenInput /\u003e\n      \u003c/RatingGroup.Control\u003e\n    \u003c/RatingGroup.Root\u003e\n    \u003cbutton type=\"submit\" className={button.Root}\u003e\n      Submit\n    \u003c/button\u003e\n  \u003c/form\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { RatingGroup } from '@ark-ui/solid/rating-group'\nimport { StarIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { Index } from 'solid-js'\nimport styles from 'styles/rating-group.module.css'\n\nexport const FormUsage = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cRatingGroup.Root class={styles.Root} name=\"my-rating\" defaultValue={3}\u003e\n    \u003cRatingGroup.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/RatingGroup.Label\u003e\n    \u003cRatingGroup.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n      \u003cRatingGroup.Context\u003e\n        {(context) =\u003e (\n          \u003cIndex each={context().items}\u003e\n            {(item) =\u003e (\n              \u003cRatingGroup.Item class={styles.Item} index={item()}\u003e\n                \u003cRatingGroup.ItemContext\u003e\n                  {(itemContext) =\u003e (\n                    \u003cspan class={styles.ItemIndicator} data-highlighted={itemContext().highlighted ? '' : undefined}\u003e\n                      \u003cStarIcon data-bg=\"\" /\u003e\n                      \u003cStarIcon data-fg=\"\" fill=\"currentColor\" /\u003e\n                    \u003c/span\u003e\n                  )}\n                \u003c/RatingGroup.ItemContext\u003e\n              \u003c/RatingGroup.Item\u003e\n            )}\n          \u003c/Index\u003e\n        )}\n      \u003c/RatingGroup.Context\u003e\n      \u003cRatingGroup.HiddenInput /\u003e\n    \u003c/RatingGroup.Control\u003e\n  \u003c/RatingGroup.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { RatingGroup } from '@ark-ui/vue/rating-group'\nimport { StarIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport styles from 'styles/rating-group.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cRatingGroup.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" name=\"my-rating\" :default-value=\"3\"\u003e\n    \u003cRatingGroup.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003eLabel\u003c/RatingGroup.Label\u003e\n    \u003cRatingGroup.Control :class=\"styles.Control\"\u003e\n      \u003cRatingGroup.Context v-slot=\"{ items }\"\u003e\n        \u003cRatingGroup.Item v-for=\"item in items\" :key=\"item\" :class=\"styles.Item\" :index=\"item\"\u003e\n          \u003cRatingGroup.ItemContext v-slot=\"{ highlighted }\"\u003e\n            \u003cspan :class=\"styles.ItemIndicator\" :data-highlighted=\"highlighted ? '' : undefined\"\u003e\n              \u003cStarIcon data-bg=\"\" /\u003e\n              \u003cStarIcon data-fg=\"\" fill=\"currentColor\" /\u003e\n            \u003c/span\u003e\n          \u003c/RatingGroup.ItemContext\u003e\n        \u003c/RatingGroup.Item\u003e\n      \u003c/RatingGroup.Context\u003e\n      \u003cRatingGroup.HiddenInput /\u003e\n    \u003c/RatingGroup.Control\u003e\n  \u003c/RatingGroup.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { RatingGroup } from '@ark-ui/svelte/rating-group'\n  import { StarIcon } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import styles from 'styles/rating-group.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cRatingGroup.Root class={styles.Root} name=\"my-rating\" defaultValue={3}\u003e\n  \u003cRatingGroup.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/RatingGroup.Label\u003e\n  \u003cRatingGroup.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n    \u003cRatingGroup.Context\u003e\n      {#snippet render(ratingGroup)}\n        {#each ratingGroup().items as item}\n          \u003cRatingGroup.Item class={styles.Item} index={item}\u003e\n            \u003cRatingGroup.ItemContext\u003e\n              {#snippet render(itemState)}\n                \u003cspan class={styles.ItemIndicator} data-highlighted={itemState().highlighted ? '' : undefined}\u003e\n                  \u003cStarIcon data-bg=\"\" /\u003e\n                  \u003cStarIcon data-fg=\"\" fill=\"currentColor\" /\u003e\n                \u003c/span\u003e\n              {/snippet}\n            \u003c/RatingGroup.ItemContext\u003e\n          \u003c/RatingGroup.Item\u003e\n        {/each}\n      {/snippet}\n    \u003c/RatingGroup.Context\u003e\n    \u003cRatingGroup.HiddenInput /\u003e\n  \u003c/RatingGroup.Control\u003e\n\u003c/RatingGroup.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Disabled\n\nTo make the rating group disabled, set the `disabled` prop to `true`.\n\n**Example: disabled**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { RatingGroup } from '@ark-ui/react/rating-group'\nimport { StarIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport styles from 'styles/rating-group.module.css'\n\nexport const Disabled = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cRatingGroup.Root className={styles.Root} defaultValue={3} disabled\u003e\n    \u003cRatingGroup.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/RatingGroup.Label\u003e\n    \u003cRatingGroup.Control className={styles.Control}\u003e\n      \u003cRatingGroup.Context\u003e\n        {({ items }) =\u003e\n          items.map((item) =\u003e (\n            \u003cRatingGroup.Item className={styles.Item} key={item} index={item}\u003e\n              \u003cRatingGroup.ItemContext\u003e\n                {({ highlighted }) =\u003e (\n                  \u003cspan className={styles.ItemIndicator} data-highlighted={highlighted ? '' : undefined}\u003e\n                    \u003cStarIcon data-bg=\"\" /\u003e\n                    \u003cStarIcon data-fg=\"\" fill=\"currentColor\" /\u003e\n                  \u003c/span\u003e\n                )}\n              \u003c/RatingGroup.ItemContext\u003e\n            \u003c/RatingGroup.Item\u003e\n          ))\n        }\n      \u003c/RatingGroup.Context\u003e\n      \u003cRatingGroup.HiddenInput /\u003e\n    \u003c/RatingGroup.Control\u003e\n  \u003c/RatingGroup.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { RatingGroup } from '@ark-ui/solid/rating-group'\nimport { StarIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { Index } from 'solid-js'\nimport styles from 'styles/rating-group.module.css'\n\nexport const Disabled = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cRatingGroup.Root class={styles.Root} defaultValue={3} disabled\u003e\n    \u003cRatingGroup.Label class={styles.Label}\u003eLabel\u003c/RatingGroup.Label\u003e\n    \u003cRatingGroup.Control class={styles.Control}\u003e\n      \u003cRatingGroup.Context\u003e\n        {(context) =\u003e (\n          \u003cIndex each={context().items}\u003e\n            {(item) =\u003e (\n              \u003cRatingGroup.Item class={styles.Item} index={item()}\u003e\n                \u003cRatingGroup.ItemContext\u003e\n                  {(itemContext) =\u003e (\n                    \u003cspan class={styles.ItemIndicator} data-highlighted={itemContext().highlighted ? '' : undefined}\u003e\n                      \u003cStarIcon data-bg=\"\" /\u003e\n                      \u003cStarIcon data-fg=\"\" fill=\"currentColor\" /\u003e\n                    \u003c/span\u003e\n                  )}\n                \u003c/RatingGroup.ItemContext\u003e\n              \u003c/RatingGroup.Item\u003e\n            )}\n          \u003c/Index\u003e\n        )}\n      \u003c/RatingGroup.Context\u003e\n      \u003cRatingGroup.HiddenInput /\u003e\n    \u003c/RatingGroup.Control\u003e\n  \u003c/RatingGroup.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { RatingGroup } from '@ark-ui/vue/rating-group'\nimport { StarIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport styles from 'styles/rating-group.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cRatingGroup.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" :default-value=\"3\" disabled\u003e\n    \u003cRatingGroup.Label :class=\"styles.Label\"\u003eLabel\u003c/RatingGroup.Label\u003e\n    \u003cRatingGroup.Control :class=\"styles.Control\"\u003e\n      \u003cRatingGroup.Context v-slot=\"{ items }\"\u003e\n        \u003cRatingGroup.Item v-for=\"item in items\" :key=\"item\" :class=\"styles.Item\" :index=\"item\"\u003e\n          \u003cRatingGroup.ItemContext v-slot=\"{ highlighted }\"\u003e\n            \u003cspan :class=\"styles.ItemIndicator\" :data-highlighted=\"highlighted ? Useful for composition. |\n| `name` | `string` | No | The name attribute of the rating element (used in forms). |\n| `onHoverChange` | `(details: HoverChangeDetails) =\u003e void` | No | Function to be called when the rating value is hovered. |\n| `onValueChange` | `(details: ValueChangeDetails) =\u003e void` | No | Function to be called when the rating value changes. |\n| `readOnly` | `boolean` | No | Whether the rating is readonly. |\n| `required` | `boolean` | No | Whether the rating is required. |\n| `translations` | `IntlTranslations` | No | Specifies the localized strings that identifies the accessibility elements and their states |\n| `value` | `number` | No | The controlled value of the rating |\n\n\n**Control Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description total number of ratings |\n| `items` | `number[]` | The array of rating values. Returns an array of numbers from 1 to the max value. |\n| `getItemState` | `(props: ItemProps) =\u003e ItemState` | Returns the state of a rating item |\n\n\n## Accessibility\n\n### Keyboard
